 uttar pradesh homeguard association kaaphi dinon se apane dainik vetan ko lekar sangharsh kar rahaa he
 In 2016, the Supreme Court in one of its orders said that the salary of home guards working in Punjab and Haryana should be equal to the salary of police constables
 uske baad disambar 2016 main uttar pradesh homeguard association ne elahabaad hoicourt main ek pitishan daayar kii thi jisamen supreme court kaa hawala dete hue kaha gaya ki uttar pradesh ke homegordon ko police consteble ke baraabar vetan milanaa chahie
 The Allahabad High Court gave a judgment in favor of the Home Guard Association
 phir uttar pradesh sarkaar iske khilaaf supreme court pahunchi
 At that time there was Akhilesh Yadav government in Uttar Pradesh
 supreme court main cese chal rahaa tha
 In 2017, the government changed in Uttar Pradesh
 bijepi kii sarkaar bani or yogi adityanath mukhyamantri bane
 After becoming the Chief Minister, Yogi Adityanath increased the daily salary of the Home Guards from 375 to 500 rupees
 puraane cese main supreme court ne 30 july 2019 ko apane aadesh main kaha ki uttar pradesh ke homegordon kaa vetan police carmik ke nunatam vetan ke baraabar ho
 Then the government of Uttar Pradesh decided to increase the salary of home guards (UP Home Guards) from Rs 500 to Rs 672 daily
 lekin ab bajet kaa kami dikhaate hue duty kam kar di

 agar sarkaar nahin maani to andolan karenge

 a post shared by Akshay Kumar (@akshaykumar) on Feb 8, 2018 at 1:51am PST Amendments have been made to the Constitution from time to time as and when required
 vidhaayini sabha main kisi vidheyak main parivartan, sudhaar athwa use nirdosh banane kii prakriya ko 'sanshodhan' kaha jaataa he
 This word is also used for the process of rectification of a proposal of a House or Committee
 kisi bhi desh kaa samvidhan kitni hi saavdhaanee se banaaya jaae, kintu manushya kii kalpana shakti kii seemaa bandhi hui he
 1
 pehla sanshodhan (1951):iske madhyam se swatantraaa, samanta evam sampatti se sambandhit moulik adhikaron ko lagu kiye jane sambandhi kuch vyavhaarik kathinaaiyon ko dur karne kaa prayaas kiya gaya
 It provided for proper restrictions on the basic rights of speech and expression
 saath hi, is sanshodhan dwaara samvidhan main naunvi anusuchee ko joda gaya, jisamen ullikhit kanoonon ko sarvocch nyaayalay ke nyaayik punarvilokan kii shaktiyon ke antargat pariksha nahin kii ja sakati he
 2
 doosraa sanshodhan (1952):iske antargat 1951 kii janaganana ke aadhaar par lok sabha main pratinidhitiv ko punarvyavasthit kiya gaya
 3
 teesraa sanshodhan (1954):antargat saatvin anusuchee ko samavarti suchi kii 33veen pravishti ke sthaan par khadyann, pashuon ke liye chaara, kaccha kapaas, jute aadi ko rakhaa gaya, jiske utpaadan evam aapurti ko lokhit main samajhane par sarkaar us par niyantran laga sakati he
 4
 chauthaa sanshodhan (1955):iske antargat vyaktigat sampatti ko lokhit main rajya dwaara hastgat kiye jane kii sthiti main, nyaayalay isaki kshatipurti ke sambandh main pariksha nahin kar sakati
 5
 paanchavaa sanshodhan (1955):is sanshodhan main anuchhed 3 main sanshodhan kiya gaya, jisamen raashtrapati ko yah shakti di gai ki vah rajya vidhaan- mandalon dwaara apane-apane rajyon ke kshetra, simaaon aadi par prabhaav daalane vaali prastaavit kendriya vidhiyon ke bare main apane vichaar bhejne ke liye koi samay-seemaa nirdhaarit kar sakate hai
 6
 chatha sanshodhan (1956):is sanshodhan dwaara saatvin anusuchee ke sangh suchi main parivartan kar antarraji bikri kar ke antargat kuch vastuon par centre ko kar lagane kaa adhikaar diya gaya he
 7
 santava sanshodhan (1956):is sanshodhan dwaara bhashiya aadhaar par rajyon kaa punargathan kiya gaya, jisamen agali teen shreniyon main rajyon ke vargeekaran ko samaapt karte hue rajyon evam centre shasit pradeshon main unhen vibhajit kiya gaya
 Also, according to them, the seats in the central and state legislatures were rearranged
 8
 Eighth Amendment (1959): Under this, the provisions relating to reservation of Scheduled Castes, Scheduled Tribes and anglo-indian Communities in the following Houses of the Center and States were extended for ten years i
e
 1970
 9
 Ninth Amendment (1960): By this, the first schedule of the Constitution was changed and according to the terms of the 1958 treaty between India and Pakistan, the areas of Berubari, Khulna etc
 were given to Pakistan
 10
 Tenth Amendment (1961): Under this, the former Portuguese inter-regions Dadar and Nagar Haveli were included in India and given the status of Union Territory
 11
 11th Amendment (1962): Under this, the joint session of both the Houses was called in this context by changing the provisions of the election of the Vice President
 saath hi yah bhi nirdhaarit kii nirvaachak mandal main pad kii riktata ke aadhaar par raashtrapati yaa uparashtrapati ke nirvachan ko chunauti nahin di ja sakati
 12
 12waan sanshodhan (1962):iske antargat samvidhan kii pratham anusuchee main sanshodhan kar goa, daman evam div ko bharat main centreshasit pradesh ke rup main shaamil kar liya gaya
 13
 13waan sanshodhan (1962):iske antargat nagaland ke sambandh main vishesh praavdhaan apanaakar use ek rajya kaa darja de diya gaya
 14
 14waan sanshodhan (1963):iske dwaara centre shasit pradesh ke rup main puducheri ko bharat main shaamil kiya gaya
 Simultaneously, Legislative Councils and Council of Ministers were established in Himachal Pradesh, Manipur, Tripura, Goa, Daman and Diu and Puducherry Union Territories
 15
 15th Amendment (1963): Under this, the age of discharge of High Court judges was increased from 60 to 62 years and provisions were made for appointment of retired judges to High Court
 16
 16th Amendment (1963): It made provisions to impose certain restrictions on fundamental rights in the interest of the sovereignty and integrity of the country and also changed the third schedule and added 'I will maintain India's independence and integrity' under oath
 Gone
 17
 17th Amendment (1964): Further amending property rights, some other land reform provisions were placed in the Ninth Schedule, whose validity could not be tested by the Supreme Court
 18
 18th Amendment (1966): Under this, Punjabi speaking area was constituted as Punjab and Hindi speaking area as Haryana while reorganizing Punjab on linguistic basis

 The Railways Ministry's decision to provide head champ (massage) and foot massage for passengers in any of the 39 trains starting from Indore (indore) in Madhya Pradesh (madhya Pradesh) is happy, but their To say that the time of champi and massage is low and the rates are kept high
 rail mantralay ne do din pehle hi indore se chalane vaali 39 gadiyon main sir kii champi or pairon kii maalish kii yojana ko manjuuri di he
 This approval has been given under the new Innovative non-fair Revenue Idea Scheme (NINFRIS) policy
 is yojana main shaamil gadiyon main teen se paanch maalish karne vaale uplabdh rahenge
 This massage will be provided to passengers in reserved and air-conditioned coaches
 railway sutron kaa kahana he ki maalish suvidha lene ke evaj main yatri ko 100 rupee se 300 rupee tak kaa bhugtan karnaa hoga
 The duration of the massage will be between 15 and 20 minutes
